#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

  ${MODULE_NAME}.py

    foreach(item IN LISTS INPUTS)
        message(STATUS ${item})
        if (WIN32)
            add_custom_command(
                TARGET ${MODULE_NAME} PRE_BUILD
                COMMAND ${CMAKE_COMMAND} -E copy "${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}\\${item}" "%userprofile%\\MSlesion_database\\${item}"
                DEPENDS "${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}\\${item}"
                )
        endif (WIN32)
        if (UNIX)
            add_custom_command(
                #TARGET ${MODULE_NAME} PRE_BUILD
		OUTPUT "~/${item}"
                COMMAND ${CMAKE_COMMAND} -E copy "${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/${item}" "~/${item}"
                DEPENDS "${CMAKE_CURRENT_SOURCE_DIR}/${item}"
                )
        endif (UNIX)
    endforeach()
endif()
